\DoxyCodeLine{87   \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_1_1internal_1_1compiler_1_1turboshaft_a1de7e1dbb8fccce9f24212ad1cd9487aace33abc6bad5986adf881f3c0e010b45}{kGotoEliminated}} = 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// The conditional GotoIf/GotoIfNot would never be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{88                          \textcolor{comment}{// executed and only the fallthrough path remains.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{89   \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_1_1internal_1_1compiler_1_1turboshaft_a1de7e1dbb8fccce9f24212ad1cd9487aa4112acb0669c771b5a3f76ac046f521e}{kBranch}} = 3            \textcolor{comment}{// The conditional Goto became a branch.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{90 }
\DoxyCodeLine{91   \textcolor{comment}{// Some examples of this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{92   \textcolor{comment}{//   GotoIf(true, dst)     ===> kGotoDestination}}
\DoxyCodeLine{93   \textcolor{comment}{//   GotoIf(false, dst)    ===> kGotoEliminated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{94   \textcolor{comment}{//   GotoIf(var, dst)      ===> kBranch}}
\DoxyCodeLine{95   \textcolor{comment}{//   GotoIfNot(true, dst)  ===> kGotoEliminated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{96   \textcolor{comment}{//   GotoIfNot(false, dst) ===> kGotoDestination}}
\DoxyCodeLine{97   \textcolor{comment}{//   GotoIfNot(var, dst)   ===> kBranch}}
\DoxyCodeLine{98 \};}
